### Cloudinary WordPress Plugin Quick Start

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/wordpress_integration

A step-by-step guide to get started with the Cloudinary WordPress plugin, from account setup to media synchronization and CDN delivery.

```Markdown
1. Sign up for a Cloudinary account or log in to your existing account.
2. Install the Cloudinary WordPress plugin from the WordPress plugin directory.
3. Complete the setup wizard, following the instructions to add your connection string and select your sync and optimization settings.
4. Your existing media will begin syncing with Cloudinary and your media URLs will be updated to enable optimized media and fast delivery via CDN.
5. That's it! Sit back and enjoy your improved site performance and greater user experience. You can keep an eye on your bandwidth savings and usage via the plugin dashboard.
```

### Cloudinary Developer Kickstart

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/product_environment_settings

Step-by-step guide for developers to register, find credentials, optimize pages, perform transformations, and set up their first SDK project.

```Developer Guide
Step 1: Register and find credentials
Step 2: Load pages faster with optimization
Step 3: Your first transformations
```

### Cloudinary Onboarding Resources

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/onboarding_resources

Resources for getting started with Cloudinary, including developer kickstart, SDK quick starts, try-it tools, video tutorials, service architecture, FAQs, and migration guides.

```APIDOC
Onboarding Resources:
  Developer kickstart: Get started quickly with Cloudinary features.
  SDK quick start: Guides for integrating Cloudinary SDKs.
  Try it: Use code explorers and demo apps for hands-on experience.
  Video tutorial library: Learn through video content.

Service Information:
  Service Introduction: Details on service architecture, asset storage, security, and add-ons.
  Onboarding FAQ: Common questions for new Cloudinary users.
  Enterprise Onboarding FAQ: Specific questions for enterprise plan users.
  Migration Guide: Methods for migrating existing assets to Cloudinary.
  Glossary: Definitions of Cloudinary terms and concepts.
```

```APIDOC
  Step 4: Resize transformations
  Step 5: Set up and run your first SDK project
  Congrats! You're ready to code!
```

### Install and Load Cloudinary Go SDK

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/go_configuration_tutorial

This snippet shows how to install the `godotenv` library, load credentials from a `.env` file, and initialize the Cloudinary client in Go.

```Go
go get github.com/joho/godotenv
```

```Go
import {
    "github.com/cloudinary/cloudinary-go/v2"
    "github.com/joho/godotenv"
}

func main() {
    err := godotenv.Load()
    if err != nil {
        log.Fatalf("Error loading .env file: %v", err)
    }
    cld, err := cloudinary.New()
    if err != nil {
        log.Fatalf("failed to initialize Cloudinary client: %v", err)
    }
}
```

### Image & Video APIs Get Started

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/get_started_with_the_cli_tutorial

An overview and initial steps for using Cloudinary's Image & Video APIs, including registration and credential retrieval.

```APIDOC
Image & Video APIs - Get Started:

This section guides new users through the initial setup for Cloudinary's Image & Video APIs.

Key Steps:
1.  **Register and Find Credentials:**
    *   Sign up for a Cloudinary account.
    *   Locate your Cloud Name, API Key, and API Secret in the dashboard.
    *   These credentials are required for authentication with the APIs and SDKs.

2.  **Developer Kickstart:**
    *   **Step 1: Register and find credentials** (Covered above).
    *   **Step 2: Load pages faster with optimization:** Learn about Cloudinary's automatic image optimization and delivery.
    *   **Step 3: Your first transformations:** Basic examples of resizing and cropping.
    *   **Step 4: Resize transformations:** Detailed guide on various resizing techniques.
    *   **Step 5: Set up and run your first SDK project:** Instructions for integrating Cloudinary into your chosen development environment.

3.  **SDK Quick Starts:** Links to quick start guides for various programming languages and frameworks.

4.  **Try it!**
    *   **Code explorers:** Interactive tools to experiment with transformations.
    *   **Feature demos:** Live examples showcasing Cloudinary's capabilities.
    *   **Postman collections:** Pre-configured requests for testing API endpoints.

5.  **MCP servers and LLM tools (Beta):** Information on advanced media processing and AI features.

6.  **Video tutorial library:** Access to video resources covering various aspects of Cloudinary usage.

Related Sections:
- Guides
- References
- SDKs
```

### Cloudinary Ruby/Rails SDK Quick Start

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/rails_integration

Get your first Ruby/Rails SDK project up and running in approximately 5 minutes. This quick start guide covers the essential steps for integration.

```Ruby
require 'cloudinary'

Cloudinary.config do |config|
  config.cloud_name = 'your_cloud_name'
  config.api_key = 'your_api_key'
  config.api_secret = 'your_api_secret'
  config.cdn_subdomain = true
end
```

### Image & Video APIs Get Started

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/get_started_with_transformations_tutorials

An overview and initial steps for using Cloudinary's Image & Video APIs, including registration and credential retrieval.

```APIDOC
Image & Video APIs - Get Started:

This section guides new users through the initial setup for Cloudinary's Image & Video APIs.

Key Steps:
1.  **Register and Find Credentials:**
    *   Sign up for a Cloudinary account.
    *   Locate your Cloud Name, API Key, and API Secret in the dashboard.
    *   These credentials are required for authentication with the APIs and SDKs.

2.  **Developer Kickstart:**
    *   **Step 1: Register and find credentials** (Covered above).
    *   **Step 2: Load pages faster with optimization:** Learn about Cloudinary's automatic image optimization and delivery.
    *   **Step 3: Your first transformations:** Basic examples of resizing and cropping.
    *   **Step 4: Resize transformations:** Detailed guide on various resizing techniques.
    *   **Step 5: Set up and run your first SDK project:** Instructions for integrating Cloudinary into your chosen development environment.

3.  **SDK Quick Starts:** Links to quick start guides for various programming languages and frameworks.

4.  **Try it!**
    *   **Code explorers:** Interactive tools to experiment with transformations.
    *   **Feature demos:** Live examples showcasing Cloudinary's capabilities.
    *   **Postman collections:** Pre-configured requests for testing API endpoints.

5.  **MCP servers and LLM tools (Beta):** Information on advanced media processing and AI features.

6.  **Video tutorial library:** Access to video resources covering various aspects of Cloudinary usage.

Related Sections:
- Guides
- References
- SDKs
```

### Signed Multi-File Upload Setup

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/client_side_uploading

Provides setup instructions for a signed multi-file upload example, including installing dependencies, configuring API keys in `config.js`, and running the Node.js server.

```Shell
1. Install all dependencies from the top level:
npm install

2. Open **signed-uploads/public/js/config.js**
3. Set `cloud_name`, `api_key` and `api_secret` with the corresponding account details from the API Keys page of the Console Settings.

4. Run the app to start the server:
node signed-uploads/app.js

The response should be:
Server is up on http://localhost:3000

5. Open `http://localhost:3000` in a browser.
```

### Perception Point Malware Detection Add-on Setup

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/perception_point_malware_detection_addon

Steps to get started with the Perception Point Malware Detection add-on for Cloudinary. This includes account requirements, add-on registration, and guidance on using SDKs for integration.

```APIDOC
Getting Started with Perception Point Malware Detection Add-on:

Prerequisites:
  - A Cloudinary account. Sign up for a free account if you don't have one.

Registration:
  1. Log in to your Cloudinary account.
  2. Navigate to the Add-ons page.
  3. Register for the Perception Point Malware Detection add-on.
     Refer to 'Registering for add-ons' for detailed information.

SDK Integration:
  - Many examples utilize Cloudinary SDKs. Consult the relevant SDK guide for installation and configuration details.

New to Cloudinary?
  - Consider the Developer Kickstart for a hands-on introduction to Cloudinary features.
```

### Image & Video APIs Get Started

Source: https://cloudinary.com/documentation/dev_kickstart_acct_setup

An overview and initial steps for using Cloudinary's Image & Video APIs, including registration and credential retrieval.

```APIDOC
Image & Video APIs - Get Started:

This section guides new users through the initial setup for Cloudinary's Image & Video APIs.

Key Steps:
1.  **Register and Find Credentials:**
    *   Sign up for a Cloudinary account.
    *   Locate your Cloud Name, API Key, and API Secret in the dashboard.
    *   These credentials are required for authentication with the APIs and SDKs.

2.  **Developer Kickstart:**
    *   **Step 1: Register and find credentials** (Covered above).
    *   **Step 2: Load pages faster with optimization:** Learn about Cloudinary's automatic image optimization and delivery.
    *   **Step 3: Your first transformations:** Basic examples of resizing and cropping.
    *   **Step 4: Resize transformations:** Detailed guide on various resizing techniques.
    *   **Step 5: Set up and run your first SDK project:** Instructions for integrating Cloudinary into your chosen development environment.

3.  **SDK Quick Starts:** Links to quick start guides for various programming languages and frameworks.

4.  **Try it!**
    *   **Code explorers:** Interactive tools to experiment with transformations.
    *   **Feature demos:** Live examples showcasing Cloudinary's capabilities.
    *   **Postman collections:** Pre-configured requests for testing API endpoints.

5.  **MCP servers and LLM tools (Beta):** Information on advanced media processing and AI features.

6.  **Video tutorial library:** Access to video resources covering various aspects of Cloudinary usage.

Related Sections:
- Guides
- References
- SDKs
```

--------------------------------
